if [[ -z $toolchain ]]; then
  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((i=${toolchain#1.}, c=($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6, i+9*i*(10*i<=c)+90*i*(100*i<=c)))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=git >> $GITHUB_ENV
  fi

if [[ -z $toolchain ]]; then
  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((i=${toolchain#1.}, c=($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6, i+9*i*(10*i<=c)+90*i*(100*i<=c)))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

  fi

[CI/Rust stable-3            ] ⭐ Run Main : enable Cargo sparse registry
# implemented in 1.66, stabilized in 1.68, made default in 1.70
if [ -z "${CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL+set}" -o -f "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol ]; then
  if rustc +stable --version --verbose | grep -q '^release: 1\.6[89]\.'; then
    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=sparse >> $GITHUB_ENV
  elif rustc +stable --version --verbose | grep -q '^release: 1\.6[67]\.'; then
    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=git >> $GITHUB_ENV
  fi
fi

    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=sparse >> $GITHUB_ENV
  elif rustc +nightly --version --verbose | grep -q '^release: 1\.6[67]\.'; then
    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=git >> $GITHUB_ENV
  fi
fi

  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else

else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

if [[ -z $toolchain ]]; then
  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((i=${toolchain#1.}, c=($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6, i+9*i*(10*i<=c)+90*i*(100*i<=c)))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

if [[ -z $toolchain ]]; then
  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((i=${toolchain#1.}, c=($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6, i+9*i*(10*i<=c)+90*i*(100*i<=c)))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true

  fi
fi

if [[ -z $toolchain ]]; then
  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((i=${toolchain#1.}, c=($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6, i+9*i*(10*i<=c)+90*i*(100*i<=c)))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

# implemented in 1.66, stabilized in 1.68, made default in 1.70
if [ -z "${CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL+set}" -o -f "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol ]; then
  if rustc +nightly --version --verbose | grep -q '^release: 1\.6[89]\.'; then
    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=sparse >> $GITHUB_ENV
  elif rustc +nightly --version --verbose | grep -q '^release: 1\.6[67]\.'; then
    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=git >> $GITHUB_ENV
  fi
fi

if [[ -z $toolchain ]]; then
  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((i=${toolchain#1.}, c=($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6, i+9*i*(10*i<=c)+90*i*(100*i<=c)))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

if [[ -z $toolchain ]]; then
  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((i=${toolchain#1.}, c=($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6, i+9*i*(10*i<=c)+90*i*(100*i<=c)))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

  # GitHub does not enforce `required: true` inputs itself. https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/1070
  echo "'toolchain' is a required input" >&2
  exit 1
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' '[0-9]+' '(year|month|week|day)s?' 'ago$ ]]; then
  if [[ Linux == macOS ]]; then
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date -v-$(sed 's/stable \([0-9]*\) \(.\).*/\1\2/' <<< $toolchain) +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  else
    echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date --date "${toolchain#stable }" +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
  fi
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^stable' 'minus' '[0-9]+' 'releases?$ ]]; then
  echo "toolchain=1.$((($(date +%s)/60/60/24-16569)/7/6-${toolchain//[^0-9]/}))" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
elif [[ $toolchain =~ ^1\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then

else
  echo "toolchain=$toolchain" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
fi

# implemented in 1.66, stabilized in 1.68, made default in 1.70
if [ -z "${CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL+set}" -o -f "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol ]; then
  if rustc +nightly --version --verbose | grep -q '^release: 1\.6[89]\.'; then
    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=sparse >> $GITHUB_ENV
  elif rustc +nightly --version --verbose | grep -q '^release: 1\.6[67]\.'; then
    touch "/tmp"/.implicit_cargo_registries_crates_io_protocol || true
    echo CARGO_REGISTRIES_CRATES_IO_PROTOCOL=git >> $GITHUB_ENV
  fi
fi
